Command to join channels #foo and</div><div class="line" id="LC905">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#bar.</div><div class="line" id="LC906">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC907">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;JOIN 0                          ; Leave all currently joined</div><div class="line" id="LC908">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channels.</div><div class="line" id="LC909">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC910">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:WiZ!jto@tolsun.oulu.fi JOIN #Twilight_zone ; JOIN message from WiZ</div><div class="line" id="LC911">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;on channel #Twilight_zone</div><div class="line" id="LC912">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC913">3.2.2 Part message</div><div class="line" id="LC914">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC915">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: PART</div><div class="line" id="LC916">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;channel&gt; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;channel&gt; ) [ &lt;Part Message&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC917">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC918">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The PART command causes the user sending the message to be removed</div><div class="line" id="LC919">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from the list of active members for all given channels listed in the</div><div class="line" id="LC920">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;parameter string.  If a &quot;Part Message&quot; is given, this will be sent</div><div class="line" id="LC921">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;instead of the default message, the nickname.  This request is always</div><div class="line" id="LC922">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;granted by the server.</div><div class="line" id="LC923">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC924">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Servers MUST be able to parse arguments in the form of a list of</div><div class="line" id="LC925">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;target, but SHOULD NOT use lists when sending PART messages to</div><div class="line" id="LC926">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;clients.</div><div class="line" id="LC927">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC928">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC929">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC930">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS              ERR_NOSUCHCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC931">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOTONCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC932">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC933">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC934">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC935">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PART #twilight_zone             ; Command to leave channel</div><div class="line" id="LC936">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;#twilight_zone&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC937">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC938">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PART #oz-ops,&amp;group5            ; Command to leave both channels</div><div class="line" id="LC939">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&amp;group5&quot; and &quot;#oz-ops&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC940">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC941">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:WiZ!jto@tolsun.oulu.fi PART #playzone :I lost</div><div class="line" id="LC942">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; User WiZ leaving channel</div><div class="line" id="LC943">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;#playzone&quot; with the message &quot;I</div><div class="line" id="LC944">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;lost&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC945">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC946">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC947">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC948">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 17]</div><div class="line" id="LC949">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC950">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC951">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC952">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC953">3.2.3 Channel mode message</div><div class="line" id="LC954">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC955">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: MODE</div><div class="line" id="LC956">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;channel&gt; *( ( &quot;-&quot; / &quot;+&quot; ) *&lt;modes&gt; *&lt;modeparams&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC957">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC958">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The MODE command is provided so that users may query and change the</div><div class="line" id="LC959">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;characteristics of a channel.  For more details on available modes</div><div class="line" id="LC960">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and their uses, see &quot;Internet Relay Chat: Channel Management&quot; [IRC-</div><div class="line" id="LC961">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CHAN].  Note that there is a maximum limit of three (3) changes per</div><div class="line" id="LC962">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command for modes that take a parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC963">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC964">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC965">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC966">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS              ERR_KEYSET</div><div class="line" id="LC967">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOCHANMODES                 ERR_CHANOPRIVSNEEDED</div><div class="line" id="LC968">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_USERNOTINCHANNEL            ERR_UNKNOWNMODE</div><div class="line" id="LC969">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_CHANNELMODEIS</div><div class="line" id="LC970">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_BANLIST                     RPL_ENDOFBANLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC971">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_EXCEPTLIST                  RPL_ENDOFEXCEPTLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC972">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_INVITELIST                  RPL_ENDOFINVITELIST</div><div class="line" id="LC973">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_UNIQOPIS</div><div class="line" id="LC974">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC975">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The following examples are given to help understanding the syntax of</div><div class="line" id="LC976">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the MODE command, but refer to modes defined in &quot;Internet Relay Chat:</div><div class="line" id="LC977">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Channel Management&quot; [IRC-CHAN].</div><div class="line" id="LC978">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC979">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC980">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC981">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MODE #Finnish +imI *!*@*.fi     ; [ &lt;topic&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1047">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1048">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The TOPIC command is used to change or view the topic of a channel.</div><div class="line" id="LC1049">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The topic for channel &lt;channel&gt; is returned if there is no &lt;topic&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1050">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;given. If the &lt;topic&gt; parameter is an empty string, the</div><div class="line" id="LC1053">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;topic for that channel will be removed.</div><div class="line" id="LC1054">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1055">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1056">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1057">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1058">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1059">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1060">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 19]</div><div class="line" id="LC1061">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1062">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1063">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1064">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1065">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1066">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1067">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS              ERR_NOTONCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC1068">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NOTOPIC                     RPL_TOPIC</div><div class="line" id="LC1069">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_CHANOPRIVSNEEDED            ERR_NOCHANMODES</div><div class="line" id="LC1070">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1071">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1072">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1073">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:WiZ!jto@tolsun.oulu.fi TOPIC #test :New topic ; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;channel&gt; ) [ &lt;target&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1089">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1090">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By using the NAMES command, a user can list all nicknames that are</div><div class="line" id="LC1091">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;visible to him. For more details on what is visible and what is not,</div><div class="line" id="LC1092">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;see &quot;Internet Relay Chat: Channel Management&quot; [IRC-CHAN].  The</div><div class="line" id="LC1093">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;channel&gt; parameter specifies which channel(s) to return information</div><div class="line" id="LC1094">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;about.  There is no error reply for bad channel names.</div><div class="line" id="LC1095">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1096">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If no &lt;channel&gt; parameter is given, a list of all channels and their</div><div class="line" id="LC1097">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;occupants is returned.  At the end of this list, a list of users who</div><div class="line" id="LC1098">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are visible but either not on any channel or not on a visible channel</div><div class="line" id="LC1099">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are listed as being on `channel&#39; &quot;*&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1100">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1101">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the &lt;target&gt; parameter is specified, the request is forwarded to</div><div class="line" id="LC1102">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;that server which will generate the reply.</div><div class="line" id="LC1103">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1104">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1105">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1106">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numerics:</div><div class="line" id="LC1107">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1108">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_TOOMANYMATCHES              ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1109">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NAMREPLY                    RPL_ENDOFNAMES</div><div class="line" id="LC1110">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1111">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1112">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1113">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1114">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1115">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1116">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 20]</div><div class="line" id="LC1117">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1118">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1119">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1120">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1121">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1122">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1123">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NAMES #twilight_zone,#42        ; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;channel&gt; ) [ &lt;target&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1133">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1134">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The list command is used to list channels and their topics.  If the</div><div class="line" id="LC1135">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;channel&gt; parameter is used, only the status of that channel is</div><div class="line" id="LC1136">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;displayed.</div><div class="line" id="LC1137">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1138">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the &lt;target&gt; parameter is specified, the request is forwarded to</div><div class="line" id="LC1139">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;that server which will generate the reply.</div><div class="line" id="LC1140">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1141">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1142">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1143">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1144">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1145">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_TOOMANYMATCHES              ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1146">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LIST                        RPL_LISTEND</div><div class="line" id="LC1147">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1148">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1149">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1150">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LIST                            ; Command to list all channels.</div><div class="line" id="LC1151">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1152">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LIST #twilight_zone,#42         ; Command to list channels</div><div class="line" id="LC1153">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#twilight_zone and #42</div><div class="line" id="LC1154">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1155">3.2.7 Invite message</div><div class="line" id="LC1156">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1157">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: INVITE</div><div class="line" id="LC1158">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;nickname&gt; &lt;channel&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1159">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1160">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The INVITE command is used to invite a user to a channel.  The</div><div class="line" id="LC1161">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;parameter &lt;nickname&gt; is the nickname of the person to be invited to</div><div class="line" id="LC1162">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the target channel &lt;channel&gt;.  There is no requirement that the</div><div class="line" id="LC1163">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channel the target user is being invited to must exist or be a valid</div><div class="line" id="LC1164">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channel.  However, if the channel exists, only members of the channel</div><div class="line" id="LC1165">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are allowed to invite other users.  When the channel has invite-only</div><div class="line" id="LC1166">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;flag set, only channel operators may issue INVITE command.</div><div class="line" id="LC1167">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1168">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1169">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1170">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1171">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1172">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 21]</div><div class="line" id="LC1173">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1174">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1175">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1176">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1177">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Only the user inviting and the user being invited will receive</div><div class="line" id="LC1178">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;notification of the invitation.  Other channel members are not</div><div class="line" id="LC1179">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;notified.  (This is unlike the MODE changes, and is occasionally the</div><div class="line" id="LC1180">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;source of trouble for users.)</div><div class="line" id="LC1181">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1182">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1183">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1184">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS              ERR_NOSUCHNICK</div><div class="line" id="LC1185">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOTONCHANNEL                ERR_USERONCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC1186">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_CHANOPRIVSNEEDED</div><div class="line" id="LC1187">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_INVITING                    RPL_AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC1188">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1189">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1190">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1191">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:Angel!wings@irc.org INVITE Wiz #Dust</div><div class="line" id="LC1192">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1193">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to WiZ when he has been</div><div class="line" id="LC1194">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;invited by user Angel to channel</div><div class="line" id="LC1195">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Dust</div><div class="line" id="LC1196">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1197">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;INVITE Wiz #Twilight_Zone       ; Command to invite WiZ to</div><div class="line" id="LC1198">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#Twilight_zone</div><div class="line" id="LC1199">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1200">3.2.8 Kick command</div><div class="line" id="LC1201">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1202">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: KICK</div><div class="line" id="LC1203">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;channel&gt; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;channel&gt; ) &lt;user&gt; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;user&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC1204">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[&lt;comment&gt;]</div><div class="line" id="LC1205">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1206">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The KICK command can be used to request the forced removal of a user</div><div class="line" id="LC1207">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from a channel.  It causes the &lt;user&gt; to PART from the &lt;channel&gt; by</div><div class="line" id="LC1208">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;force.  For the message to be syntactically correct, there MUST be</div><div class="line" id="LC1209">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;either one channel parameter and multiple user parameter, or as many</div><div class="line" id="LC1210">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channel parameters as there are user parameters.  If a &quot;comment&quot; is</div><div class="line" id="LC1211">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;given, this will be sent instead of the default message, the nickname</div><div class="line" id="LC1212">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of the user issuing the KICK.</div><div class="line" id="LC1213">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1214">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The server MUST NOT send KICK messages with multiple channels or</div><div class="line" id="LC1215">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;users to clients.  This is necessarily to maintain backward</div><div class="line" id="LC1216">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;compatibility with old client software.</div><div class="line" id="LC1217">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1218">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1219">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1220">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS              ERR_NOSUCHCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC1221">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_BADCHANMASK                 ERR_CHANOPRIVSNEEDED</div><div class="line" id="LC1222">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_USERNOTINCHANNEL            ERR_NOTONCHANNEL</div><div class="line" id="LC1223">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1224">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1225">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1226">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1227">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1228">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 22]</div><div class="line" id="LC1229">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1230">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1231">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1232">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1233">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1234">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1235">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;KICK &amp;Melbourne Matthew         ; Command to kick Matthew from</div><div class="line" id="LC1236">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&amp;Melbourne</div><div class="line" id="LC1237">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1238">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;KICK #Finnish John :Speaking English</div><div class="line" id="LC1239">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Command to kick John from #Finnish</div><div class="line" id="LC1240">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;using &quot;Speaking English&quot; as the</div><div class="line" id="LC1241">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reason (comment).</div><div class="line" id="LC1242">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1243">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:WiZ!jto@tolsun.oulu.fi KICK #Finnish John</div><div class="line" id="LC1244">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; KICK message on channel #Finnish</div><div class="line" id="LC1245">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from WiZ to remove John from channel</div><div class="line" id="LC1246">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1247">3.3 Sending messages</div><div class="line" id="LC1248">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1249">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The main purpose of the IRC protocol is to provide a base for clients</div><div class="line" id="LC1250">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to communicate with each other.  PRIVMSG, NOTICE and SQUERY</div><div class="line" id="LC1251">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(described in Section 3.5 on Service Query and Commands) are the only</div><div class="line" id="LC1252">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;messages available which actually perform delivery of a text message</div><div class="line" id="LC1253">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from one client to another - the rest just make it possible and try</div><div class="line" id="LC1254">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to ensure it happens in a reliable and structured manner.</div><div class="line" id="LC1255">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1256">3.3.1 Private messages</div><div class="line" id="LC1257">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1258">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: PRIVMSG</div><div class="line" id="LC1259">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;msgtarget&gt; &lt;text to be sent&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1260">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1261">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG is used to send private messages between users, as well as to</div><div class="line" id="LC1262">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;send messages to channels.  &lt;msgtarget&gt; is usually the nickname of</div><div class="line" id="LC1263">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the recipient of the message, or a channel name.</div><div class="line" id="LC1264">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1265">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &lt;msgtarget&gt; parameter may also be a host mask (#&lt;mask&gt;) or server</div><div class="line" id="LC1266">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mask ($&lt;mask&gt;).  In both cases the server will only send the PRIVMSG</div><div class="line" id="LC1267">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to those who have a server or host matching the mask.  The mask MUST</div><div class="line" id="LC1268">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;have at least 1 (one) &quot;.&quot; in it and no wildcards following the last</div><div class="line" id="LC1269">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;.&quot;.  This requirement exists to prevent people sending messages to</div><div class="line" id="LC1270">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;#*&quot; or &quot;$*&quot;, which would broadcast to all users.  Wildcards are the</div><div class="line" id="LC1271">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;*&#39; and &#39;?&#39;  characters.  This extension to the PRIVMSG command is</div><div class="line" id="LC1272">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;only available to operators.</div><div class="line" id="LC1273">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1274">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1275">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1276">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NORECIPIENT                 ERR_NOTEXTTOSEND</div><div class="line" id="LC1277">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_CANNOTSENDTOCHAN            ERR_NOTOPLEVEL</div><div class="line" id="LC1278">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_WILDTOPLEVEL                ERR_TOOMANYTARGETS</div><div class="line" id="LC1279">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHNICK</div><div class="line" id="LC1280">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC1281">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1282">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1283">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1284">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 23]</div><div class="line" id="LC1285">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1286">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1287">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1288">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1289">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1290">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1291">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:Angel!wings@irc.org PRIVMSG Wiz :Are you receiving this message ?</div><div class="line" id="LC1292">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message from Angel to Wiz.</div><div class="line" id="LC1293">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1294">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG Angel :yes I&#39;m receiving it !</div><div class="line" id="LC1295">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Command to send a message to Angel.</div><div class="line" id="LC1296">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1297">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG jto@tolsun.oulu.fi :Hello !</div><div class="line" id="LC1298">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Command to send a message to a user</div><div class="line" id="LC1299">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;on server tolsun.oulu.fi with</div><div class="line" id="LC1300">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;username of &quot;jto&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1301">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1302">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG kalt%millennium.stealth.net@irc.stealth.net :Are you a frog?</div><div class="line" id="LC1303">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to a user on server</div><div class="line" id="LC1304">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;irc.stealth.net with username of</div><div class="line" id="LC1305">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;kalt&quot;, and connected from the host</div><div class="line" id="LC1306">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;millennium.stealth.net.</div><div class="line" id="LC1307">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1308">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG kalt%millennium.stealth.net :Do you like cheese?</div><div class="line" id="LC1309">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to a user on the local</div><div class="line" id="LC1310">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server with username of &quot;kalt&quot;, and</div><div class="line" id="LC1311">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connected from the host</div><div class="line" id="LC1312">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;millennium.stealth.net.</div><div class="line" id="LC1313">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1314">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG Wiz!jto@tolsun.oulu.fi :Hello !</div><div class="line" id="LC1315">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to the user with nickname</div><div class="line" id="LC1316">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wiz who is connected from the host</div><div class="line" id="LC1317">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tolsun.oulu.fi and has the username</div><div class="line" id="LC1318">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;jto&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1319">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1320">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG $*.fi :Server tolsun.oulu.fi rebooting.</div><div class="line" id="LC1321">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to everyone on a server</div><div class="line" id="LC1322">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which has a name matching *.fi.</div><div class="line" id="LC1323">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1324">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG #*.edu :NSFNet is undergoing work, expect interruptions</div><div class="line" id="LC1325">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to all users who come from</div><div class="line" id="LC1326">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a host which has a name matching</div><div class="line" id="LC1327">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*.edu.</div><div class="line" id="LC1328">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1329">3.3.2 Notice</div><div class="line" id="LC1330">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1331">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: NOTICE</div><div class="line" id="LC1332">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;msgtarget&gt; &lt;text&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1333">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1334">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The NOTICE command is used similarly to PRIVMSG.  The difference</div><div class="line" id="LC1335">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;between NOTICE and PRIVMSG is that automatic replies MUST NEVER be</div><div class="line" id="LC1336">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent in response to a NOTICE message.  This rule applies to servers</div><div class="line" id="LC1337">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1338">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1339">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1340">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 24]</div><div class="line" id="LC1341">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1342">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1343">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1344">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1345">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;too - they MUST NOT send any error reply back to the client on</div><div class="line" id="LC1346">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;receipt of a notice.  The object of this rule is to avoid loops</div><div class="line" id="LC1347">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;between clients automatically sending something in response to</div><div class="line" id="LC1348">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;something it received.</div><div class="line" id="LC1349">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1350">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This command is available to services as well as users.</div><div class="line" id="LC1351">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1352">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This is typically used by services, and automatons (clients with</div><div class="line" id="LC1353">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;either an AI or other interactive program controlling their actions).</div><div class="line" id="LC1354">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1355">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;See PRIVMSG for more details on replies and examples.</div><div class="line" id="LC1356">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1357">3.4 Server queries and commands</div><div class="line" id="LC1358">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1359">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The server query group of commands has been designed to return</div><div class="line" id="LC1360">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information about any server which is connected to the network.</div><div class="line" id="LC1361">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1362">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In these queries, where a parameter appears as &lt;target&gt;, wildcard</div><div class="line" id="LC1363">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;masks are usually valid.  For each parameter, however, only one query</div><div class="line" id="LC1364">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and set of replies is to be generated.  In most cases, if a nickname</div><div class="line" id="LC1365">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is given, it will mean the server to which the user is connected.</div><div class="line" id="LC1366">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1367">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;These messages typically have little value for services, it is</div><div class="line" id="LC1368">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;therefore RECOMMENDED to forbid services from using them.</div><div class="line" id="LC1369">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1370">3.4.1 Motd message</div><div class="line" id="LC1371">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1372">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: MOTD</div><div class="line" id="LC1373">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1374">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1375">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The MOTD command is used to get the &quot;Message Of The Day&quot; of the given</div><div class="line" id="LC1376">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server, or current server if &lt;target&gt; is omitted.</div><div class="line" id="LC1377">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1378">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1379">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1380">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1381">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_MOTDSTART                   RPL_MOTD</div><div class="line" id="LC1382">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFMOTD                   ERR_NOMOTD</div><div class="line" id="LC1383">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1384">3.4.2 Lusers message</div><div class="line" id="LC1385">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1386">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: LUSERS</div><div class="line" id="LC1387">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;mask&gt; [ &lt;target&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1388">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1389">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The LUSERS command is used to get statistics about the size of the</div><div class="line" id="LC1390">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;IRC network.  If no parameter is given, the reply will be about the</div><div class="line" id="LC1391">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;whole net.  If a &lt;mask&gt; is specified, then the reply will only</div><div class="line" id="LC1392">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1393">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1394">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1395">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1396">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 25]</div><div class="line" id="LC1397">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1398">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1399">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1400">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1401">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;concern the part of the network formed by the servers matching the</div><div class="line" id="LC1402">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mask.  Finally, if the &lt;target&gt; parameter is specified, the request</div><div class="line" id="LC1403">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is forwarded to that server which will generate the reply.</div><div class="line" id="LC1404">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1405">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1406">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1407">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1408">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1409">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSERCLIENT                 RPL_LUSEROP</div><div class="line" id="LC1410">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSERUNKOWN                 RPL_LUSERCHANNELS</div><div class="line" id="LC1411">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSERME                     ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1412">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1413">3.4.3 Version message</div><div class="line" id="LC1414">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1415">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: VERSION</div><div class="line" id="LC1416">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1417">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1418">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The VERSION command is used to query the version of the server</div><div class="line" id="LC1419">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;program.  An optional parameter &lt;target&gt; is used to query the version</div><div class="line" id="LC1420">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of the server program which a client is not directly connected to.</div><div class="line" id="LC1421">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1422">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1423">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1424">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1425">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1426">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER                RPL_VERSION</div><div class="line" id="LC1427">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1428">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1429">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1430">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;VERSION tolsun.oulu.fi          ; Command to check the version of</div><div class="line" id="LC1431">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server &quot;tolsun.oulu.fi&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1432">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1433">3.4.4 Stats message</div><div class="line" id="LC1434">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1435">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: STATS</div><div class="line" id="LC1436">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;query&gt; [ &lt;target&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1437">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1438">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The stats command is used to query statistics of certain server.  If</div><div class="line" id="LC1439">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;query&gt; parameter is omitted, only the end of stats reply is sent</div><div class="line" id="LC1440">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;back.</div><div class="line" id="LC1441">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1442">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A query may be given for any single letter which is only checked by</div><div class="line" id="LC1443">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the destination server and is otherwise passed on by intermediate</div><div class="line" id="LC1444">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;servers, ignored and unaltered.</div><div class="line" id="LC1445">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1446">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1447">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1448">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1449">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1450">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1451">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1452">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 26]</div><div class="line" id="LC1453">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1454">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1455">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1456">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1457">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except for the ones below, the list of valid queries is</div><div class="line" id="LC1458">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;implementation dependent.  The standard queries below SHOULD be</div><div class="line" id="LC1459">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;supported by the server:</div><div class="line" id="LC1460">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1461">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;l - returns a list of the server&#39;s connections, showing how</div><div class="line" id="LC1462">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;long each connection has been established and the</div><div class="line" id="LC1463">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;traffic over that connection in Kbytes and messages for</div><div class="line" id="LC1464">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each direction;</div><div class="line" id="LC1465">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;m - returns the usage count for each of commands supported</div><div class="line" id="LC1466">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by the server; commands for which the usage count is</div><div class="line" id="LC1467">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;zero MAY be omitted;</div><div class="line" id="LC1468">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;o - returns a list of configured privileged users,</div><div class="line" id="LC1469">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;operators;</div><div class="line" id="LC1470">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;u - returns a string showing how long the server has been</div><div class="line" id="LC1471">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;up.</div><div class="line" id="LC1472">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1473">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;It is also RECOMMENDED that client and server access configuration be</div><div class="line" id="LC1474">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;published this way.</div><div class="line" id="LC1475">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1476">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1477">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1478">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1479">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_STATSLINKINFO                RPL_STATSUPTIME</div><div class="line" id="LC1480">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_STATSCOMMANDS                RPL_STATSOLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC1481">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFSTATS</div><div class="line" id="LC1482">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1483">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1484">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1485">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;STATS m                         ; Command to check the command usage</div><div class="line" id="LC1486">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for the server you are connected to</div><div class="line" id="LC1487">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1488">3.4.5 Links message</div><div class="line" id="LC1489">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1490">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: LINKS</div><div class="line" id="LC1491">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ [ &lt;remote server&gt; ] &lt;server mask&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1492">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1493">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With LINKS, a user can list all servernames, which are known by the</div><div class="line" id="LC1494">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server answering the query.  The returned list of servers MUST match</div><div class="line" id="LC1495">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the mask, or if no mask is given, the full list is returned.</div><div class="line" id="LC1496">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1497">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If &lt;remote server&gt; is given in addition to &lt;server mask&gt;, the LINKS</div><div class="line" id="LC1498">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command is forwarded to the first server found that matches that name</div><div class="line" id="LC1499">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(if any), and that server is then required to answer the query.</div><div class="line" id="LC1500">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1501">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1502">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1503">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1504">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LINKS                        RPL_ENDOFLINKS</div><div class="line" id="LC1505">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1506">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1507">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1508">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 27]</div><div class="line" id="LC1509">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1510">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1511">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1512">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1513">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1514">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1515">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LINKS *.au                      ; Command to list all servers which</div><div class="line" id="LC1516">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;have a name that matches *.au;</div><div class="line" id="LC1517">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1518">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LINKS *.edu *.bu.edu            ; Command to list servers matching</div><div class="line" id="LC1519">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*.bu.edu as seen by the first server</div><div class="line" id="LC1520">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;matching *.edu.</div><div class="line" id="LC1521">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1522">3.4.6 Time message</div><div class="line" id="LC1523">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1524">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: TIME</div><div class="line" id="LC1525">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1526">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1527">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The time command is used to query local time from the specified</div><div class="line" id="LC1528">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server. If the &lt;target&gt; parameter is not given, the server receiving</div><div class="line" id="LC1529">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the command must reply to the query.</div><div class="line" id="LC1530">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1531">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1532">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1533">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1534">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1535">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER              RPL_TIME</div><div class="line" id="LC1536">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1537">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1538">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TIME tolsun.oulu.fi             ; check the time on the server</div><div class="line" id="LC1539">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;tolson.oulu.fi&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC1540">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1541">3.4.7 Connect message</div><div class="line" id="LC1542">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1543">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: CONNECT</div><div class="line" id="LC1544">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;target server&gt; &lt;port&gt; [ &lt;remote server&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1545">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1546">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The CONNECT command can be used to request a server to try to</div><div class="line" id="LC1547">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;establish a new connection to another server immediately.  CONNECT is</div><div class="line" id="LC1548">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a privileged command and SHOULD be available only to IRC Operators.</div><div class="line" id="LC1549">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If a &lt;remote server&gt; is given and its mask doesn&#39;t match name of the</div><div class="line" id="LC1550">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;parsing server, the CONNECT attempt is sent to the first match of</div><div class="line" id="LC1551">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;remote server. Otherwise the CONNECT attempt is made by the server</div><div class="line" id="LC1552">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;processing the request.</div><div class="line" id="LC1553">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1554">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The server receiving a remote CONNECT command SHOULD generate a</div><div class="line" id="LC1555">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WALLOPS message describing the source and target of the request.</div><div class="line" id="LC1556">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1557">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1558">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1559">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER              ERR_NOPRIVILEGES</div><div class="line" id="LC1560">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS</div><div class="line" id="LC1561">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1562">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1563">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1564">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 28]</div><div class="line" id="LC1565">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1566">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1567">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1568">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1569">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1570">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1571">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CONNECT tolsun.oulu.fi 6667     ; Command to attempt to connect local</div><div class="line" id="LC1572">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server to tolsun.oulu.fi on port 6667</div><div class="line" id="LC1573">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1574">3.4.8 Trace message</div><div class="line" id="LC1575">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1576">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: TRACE</div><div class="line" id="LC1577">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1578">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1579">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TRACE command is used to find the route to specific server and</div><div class="line" id="LC1580">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information about its peers.  Each server that processes this command</div><div class="line" id="LC1581">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MUST report to the sender about it.  The replies from pass-through</div><div class="line" id="LC1582">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;links form a chain, which shows route to destination.  After sending</div><div class="line" id="LC1583">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;this reply back, the query MUST be sent to the next server until</div><div class="line" id="LC1584">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;given &lt;target&gt; server is reached.</div><div class="line" id="LC1585">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1586">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TRACE command is used to find the route to specific server.  Each</div><div class="line" id="LC1587">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server that processes this message MUST tell the sender about it by</div><div class="line" id="LC1588">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sending a reply indicating it is a pass-through link, forming a chain</div><div class="line" id="LC1589">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of replies.  After sending this reply back, it MUST then send the</div><div class="line" id="LC1590">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TRACE message to the next server until given server is reached.  If</div><div class="line" id="LC1591">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the &lt;target&gt; parameter is omitted, it is RECOMMENDED that TRACE</div><div class="line" id="LC1592">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command sends a message to the sender telling which servers the local</div><div class="line" id="LC1593">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server has direct connection to.</div><div class="line" id="LC1594">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1595">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the destination given by &lt;target&gt; is an actual server, the</div><div class="line" id="LC1596">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;destination server is REQUIRED to report all servers, services and</div><div class="line" id="LC1597">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;operators which are connected to it; if the command was issued by an</div><div class="line" id="LC1598">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;operator, the server MAY also report all users which are connected to</div><div class="line" id="LC1599">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;it.  If the destination given by &lt;target&gt; is a nickname, then only a</div><div class="line" id="LC1600">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reply for that nickname is given.  If the &lt;target&gt; parameter is</div><div class="line" id="LC1601">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;omitted, it is RECOMMENDED that the TRACE command is parsed as</div><div class="line" id="LC1602">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;targeted to the processing server.</div><div class="line" id="LC1603">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1604">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1605">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1606">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1607">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1608">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1609">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1610">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the TRACE message is destined for another server, all</div><div class="line" id="LC1611">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;intermediate servers must return a RPL_TRACELINK reply to indicate</div><div class="line" id="LC1612">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;that the TRACE passed through it and where it is going next.</div><div class="line" id="LC1613">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1614">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACELINK</div><div class="line" id="LC1615">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1616">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1617">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1618">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1619">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1620">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 29]</div><div class="line" id="LC1621">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1622">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1623">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1624">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1625">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A TRACE reply may be composed of any number of the following</div><div class="line" id="LC1626">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;numeric replies.</div><div class="line" id="LC1627">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1628">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACECONNECTING           RPL_TRACEHANDSHAKE</div><div class="line" id="LC1629">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACEUNKNOWN              RPL_TRACEOPERATOR</div><div class="line" id="LC1630">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACEUSER                 RPL_TRACESERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1631">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACESERVICE              RPL_TRACENEWTYPE</div><div class="line" id="LC1632">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACECLASS                RPL_TRACELOG</div><div class="line" id="LC1633">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACEEND</div><div class="line" id="LC1634">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1635">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1636">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1637">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TRACE *.oulu.fi                 ; TRACE to a server matching</div><div class="line" id="LC1638">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*.oulu.fi</div><div class="line" id="LC1639">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1640">3.4.9 Admin command</div><div class="line" id="LC1641">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1642">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: ADMIN</div><div class="line" id="LC1643">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1644">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1645">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The admin command is used to find information about the administrator</div><div class="line" id="LC1646">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of the given server, or current server if &lt;target&gt; parameter is</div><div class="line" id="LC1647">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;omitted.  Each server MUST have the ability to forward ADMIN messages</div><div class="line" id="LC1648">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to other servers.</div><div class="line" id="LC1649">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1650">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1651">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1652">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1653">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1654">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1655">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ADMINME                   RPL_ADMINLOC1</div><div class="line" id="LC1656">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ADMINLOC2                 RPL_ADMINEMAIL</div><div class="line" id="LC1657">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1658">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1659">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1660">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ADMIN tolsun.oulu.fi            ; request an ADMIN reply from</div><div class="line" id="LC1661">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tolsun.oulu.fi</div><div class="line" id="LC1662">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1663">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ADMIN syrk                      ; ADMIN request for the server to</div><div class="line" id="LC1664">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which the user syrk is connected</div><div class="line" id="LC1665">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1666">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1667">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1668">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1669">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1670">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1671">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1672">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1673">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1674">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1675">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1676">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 30]</div><div class="line" id="LC1677">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1678">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1679">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1680">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1681">3.4.10 Info command</div><div class="line" id="LC1682">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1683">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: INFO</div><div class="line" id="LC1684">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1685">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1686">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The INFO command is REQUIRED to return information describing the</div><div class="line" id="LC1687">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server: its version, when it was compiled, the patchlevel, when it</div><div class="line" id="LC1688">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;was started, and any other miscellaneous information which may be</div><div class="line" id="LC1689">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;considered to be relevant.</div><div class="line" id="LC1690">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1691">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1692">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1693">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1694">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1695">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1696">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_INFO                      RPL_ENDOFINFO</div><div class="line" id="LC1697">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1698">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1699">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1700">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;INFO csd.bu.edu                 ; request an INFO reply from</div><div class="line" id="LC1701">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;csd.bu.edu</div><div class="line" id="LC1702">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1703">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;INFO Angel                      ; request info from the server that</div><div class="line" id="LC1704">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Angel is connected to.</div><div class="line" id="LC1705">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1706">3.5 Service Query and Commands</div><div class="line" id="LC1707">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1708">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The service query group of commands has been designed to return</div><div class="line" id="LC1709">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information about any service which is connected to the network.</div><div class="line" id="LC1710">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1711">3.5.1 Servlist message</div><div class="line" id="LC1712">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1713">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: SERVLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC1714">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;mask&gt; [ &lt;type&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1715">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1716">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SERVLIST command is used to list services currently connected to</div><div class="line" id="LC1717">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the network and visible to the user issuing the command.  The</div><div class="line" id="LC1718">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;optional parameters may be used to restrict the result of the query</div><div class="line" id="LC1719">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(to matching services names, and services type).</div><div class="line" id="LC1720">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1721">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1722">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1723">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_SERVLIST                  RPL_SERVLISTEND</div><div class="line" id="LC1724">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1725">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1726">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1727">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1728">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1729">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1730">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1731">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1732">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 31]</div><div class="line" id="LC1733">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1734">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1735">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1736">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1737">3.5.2 Squery</div><div class="line" id="LC1738">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1739">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: SQUERY</div><div class="line" id="LC1740">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;servicename&gt; &lt;text&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1741">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1742">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SQUERY command is used similarly to PRIVMSG.  The only difference</div><div class="line" id="LC1743">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is that the recipient MUST be a service.  This is the only way for a</div><div class="line" id="LC1744">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;text message to be delivered to a service.</div><div class="line" id="LC1745">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1746">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;See PRIVMSG for more details on replies and example.</div><div class="line" id="LC1747">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1748">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1749">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1750">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SQUERY irchelp :HELP privmsg</div><div class="line" id="LC1751">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to the service with</div><div class="line" id="LC1752">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;nickname irchelp.</div><div class="line" id="LC1753">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1754">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SQUERY dict@irc.fr :fr2en blaireau</div><div class="line" id="LC1755">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Message to the service with name</div><div class="line" id="LC1756">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;dict@irc.fr.</div><div class="line" id="LC1757">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1758">3.6 User based queries</div><div class="line" id="LC1759">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1760">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;User queries are a group of commands which are primarily concerned</div><div class="line" id="LC1761">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with finding details on a particular user or group users.  When using</div><div class="line" id="LC1762">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;wildcards with any of these commands, if they match, they will only</div><div class="line" id="LC1763">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return information on users who are &#39;visible&#39; to you.  The visibility</div><div class="line" id="LC1764">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of a user is determined as a combination of the user&#39;s mode and the</div><div class="line" id="LC1765">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;common set of channels you are both on.</div><div class="line" id="LC1766">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1767">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Although services SHOULD NOT be using this class of message, they are</div><div class="line" id="LC1768">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;allowed to.</div><div class="line" id="LC1769">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1770">3.6.1 Who query</div><div class="line" id="LC1771">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1772">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: WHO</div><div class="line" id="LC1773">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;mask&gt; [ &quot;o&quot; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1774">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1775">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The WHO command is used by a client to generate a query which returns</div><div class="line" id="LC1776">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a list of information which &#39;matches&#39; the &lt;mask&gt; parameter given by</div><div class="line" id="LC1777">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the client.  In the absence of the &lt;mask&gt; parameter, all visible</div><div class="line" id="LC1778">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(users who aren&#39;t invisible (user mode +i) and who don&#39;t have a</div><div class="line" id="LC1779">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;common channel with the requesting client) are listed.  The same</div><div class="line" id="LC1780">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;result can be achieved by using a &lt;mask&gt; of &quot;0&quot; or any wildcard which</div><div class="line" id="LC1781">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;will end up matching every visible user.</div><div class="line" id="LC1782">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1783">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &lt;mask&gt; passed to WHO is matched against users&#39; host, server, real</div><div class="line" id="LC1784">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;name and nickname if the channel &lt;mask&gt; cannot be found.</div><div class="line" id="LC1785">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1786">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1787">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1788">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 32]</div><div class="line" id="LC1789">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1790">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1791">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1792">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1793">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the &quot;o&quot; parameter is passed only operators are returned according</div><div class="line" id="LC1794">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to the &lt;mask&gt; supplied.</div><div class="line" id="LC1795">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1796">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1797">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1798">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1799">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_WHOREPLY                  RPL_ENDOFWHO</div><div class="line" id="LC1800">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1801">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1802">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1803">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHO *.fi                        ; Command to list all users who match</div><div class="line" id="LC1804">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;against &quot;*.fi&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1805">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1806">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHO jto* o                      ; Command to list all users with a</div><div class="line" id="LC1807">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;match against &quot;jto*&quot; if they are an</div><div class="line" id="LC1808">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;operator.</div><div class="line" id="LC1809">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1810">3.6.2 Whois query</div><div class="line" id="LC1811">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1812">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: WHOIS</div><div class="line" id="LC1813">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ] &lt;mask&gt; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;mask&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC1814">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1815">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This command is used to query information about particular user.</div><div class="line" id="LC1816">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The server will answer this command with several numeric messages</div><div class="line" id="LC1817">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;indicating different statuses of each user which matches the mask (if</div><div class="line" id="LC1818">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;you are entitled to see them).  If no wildcard is present in the</div><div class="line" id="LC1819">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;mask&gt;, any information about that nick which you are allowed to see</div><div class="line" id="LC1820">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is presented.</div><div class="line" id="LC1821">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1822">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the &lt;target&gt; parameter is specified, it sends the query to a</div><div class="line" id="LC1823">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;specific server.
