It is useful if you want to know how long the user</div><div class="line" id="LC1824">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in question has been idle as only local server (i.e., the server the</div><div class="line" id="LC1825">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;user is directly connected to) knows that information, while</div><div class="line" id="LC1826">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;everything else is globally known.</div><div class="line" id="LC1827">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1828">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1829">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1830">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1831">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1832">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER              ERR_NONICKNAMEGIVEN</div><div class="line" id="LC1833">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_WHOISUSER                 RPL_WHOISCHANNELS</div><div class="line" id="LC1834">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_WHOISCHANNELS             RPL_WHOISSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1835">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_AWAY                      RPL_WHOISOPERATOR</div><div class="line" id="LC1836">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_WHOISIDLE                 ERR_NOSUCHNICK</div><div class="line" id="LC1837">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFWHOIS</div><div class="line" id="LC1838">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1839">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1840">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1841">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1842">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1843">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1844">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 33]</div><div class="line" id="LC1845">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1846">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1847">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1848">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1849">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1850">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1851">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHOIS wiz                       ; return available user information</div><div class="line" id="LC1852">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;about nick WiZ</div><div class="line" id="LC1853">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1854">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHOIS eff.org trillian          ; ask server eff.org for user</div><div class="line" id="LC1855">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;information  about trillian</div><div class="line" id="LC1856">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1857">3.6.3 Whowas</div><div class="line" id="LC1858">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1859">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: WHOWAS</div><div class="line" id="LC1860">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;nickname&gt; *( &quot;,&quot; &lt;nickname&gt; ) [ &lt;count&gt; [ &lt;target&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1861">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1862">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whowas asks for information about a nickname which no longer exists.</div><div class="line" id="LC1863">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This may either be due to a nickname change or the user leaving IRC.</div><div class="line" id="LC1864">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In response to this query, the server searches through its nickname</div><div class="line" id="LC1865">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;history, looking for any nicks which are lexically the same (no wild</div><div class="line" id="LC1866">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;card matching here).  The history is searched backward, returning the</div><div class="line" id="LC1867">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;most recent entry first.  If there are multiple entries, up to</div><div class="line" id="LC1868">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;count&gt; replies will be returned (or all of them if no &lt;count&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1869">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;parameter is given).  If a non-positive number is passed as being</div><div class="line" id="LC1870">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;count&gt;, then a full search is done.</div><div class="line" id="LC1871">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1872">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wildcards are allowed in the &lt;target&gt; parameter.</div><div class="line" id="LC1873">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1874">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1875">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1876">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NONICKNAMEGIVEN           ERR_WASNOSUCHNICK</div><div class="line" id="LC1877">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_WHOWASUSER                RPL_WHOISSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1878">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFWHOWAS</div><div class="line" id="LC1879">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1880">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1881">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1882">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHOWAS Wiz                      ; return all information in the nick</div><div class="line" id="LC1883">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;history about nick &quot;WiZ&quot;;</div><div class="line" id="LC1884">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1885">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHOWAS Mermaid 9                ; return at most, the 9 most recent</div><div class="line" id="LC1886">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;entries in the nick history for</div><div class="line" id="LC1887">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Mermaid&quot;;</div><div class="line" id="LC1888">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1889">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHOWAS Trillian 1 *.edu         ; return the most recent history for</div><div class="line" id="LC1890">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Trillian&quot; from the first server</div><div class="line" id="LC1891">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;found to match &quot;*.edu&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC1892">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1893">3.7 Miscellaneous messages</div><div class="line" id="LC1894">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1895">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Messages in this category do not fit into any of the above categories</div><div class="line" id="LC1896">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;but are nonetheless still a part of and REQUIRED by the protocol.</div><div class="line" id="LC1897">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1898">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1899">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1900">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 34]</div><div class="line" id="LC1901">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1902">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1903">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1904">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1905">3.7.1 Kill message</div><div class="line" id="LC1906">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1907">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: KILL</div><div class="line" id="LC1908">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;nickname&gt; &lt;comment&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC1909">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1910">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The KILL command is used to cause a client-server connection to be</div><div class="line" id="LC1911">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;closed by the server which has the actual connection.  Servers</div><div class="line" id="LC1912">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;generate KILL messages on nickname collisions.  It MAY also be</div><div class="line" id="LC1913">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;available available to users who have the operator status.</div><div class="line" id="LC1914">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1915">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Clients which have automatic reconnect algorithms effectively make</div><div class="line" id="LC1916">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;this command useless since the disconnection is only brief.  It does</div><div class="line" id="LC1917">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;however break the flow of data and can be used to stop large amounts</div><div class="line" id="LC1918">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of &#39;flooding&#39; from abusive users or accidents.  Abusive users usually</div><div class="line" id="LC1919">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;don&#39;t care as they will reconnect promptly and resume their abusive</div><div class="line" id="LC1920">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;behaviour.  To prevent this command from being abused, any user may</div><div class="line" id="LC1921">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;elect to receive KILL messages generated for others to keep an &#39;eye&#39;</div><div class="line" id="LC1922">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;on would be trouble spots.</div><div class="line" id="LC1923">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1924">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In an arena where nicknames are REQUIRED to be globally unique at all</div><div class="line" id="LC1925">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;times, KILL messages are sent whenever &#39;duplicates&#39; are detected</div><div class="line" id="LC1926">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(that is an attempt to register two users with the same nickname) in</div><div class="line" id="LC1927">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the hope that both of them will disappear and only 1 reappear.</div><div class="line" id="LC1928">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1929">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When a client is removed as the result of a KILL message, the server</div><div class="line" id="LC1930">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SHOULD add the nickname to the list of unavailable nicknames in an</div><div class="line" id="LC1931">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;attempt to avoid clients to reuse this name immediately which is</div><div class="line" id="LC1932">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;usually the pattern of abusive behaviour often leading to useless</div><div class="line" id="LC1933">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;KILL loops&quot;.  See the &quot;IRC Server Protocol&quot; document [IRC-SERVER]</div><div class="line" id="LC1934">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for more information on this procedure.</div><div class="line" id="LC1935">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1936">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The comment given MUST reflect the actual reason for the KILL.  For</div><div class="line" id="LC1937">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server-generated KILLs it usually is made up of details concerning</div><div class="line" id="LC1938">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the origins of the two conflicting nicknames.  For users it is left</div><div class="line" id="LC1939">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;up to them to provide an adequate reason to satisfy others who see</div><div class="line" id="LC1940">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;it.  To prevent/discourage fake KILLs from being generated to hide</div><div class="line" id="LC1941">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the identify of the KILLer, the comment also shows a &#39;kill-path&#39;</div><div class="line" id="LC1942">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which is updated by each server it passes through, each prepending</div><div class="line" id="LC1943">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;its name to the path.</div><div class="line" id="LC1944">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1945">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1946">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1947">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOPRIVILEGES              ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS</div><div class="line" id="LC1948">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHNICK                ERR_CANTKILLSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1949">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1950">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1951">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1952">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1953">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1954">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1955">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1956">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 35]</div><div class="line" id="LC1957">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1958">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC1959">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1960">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1961">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOTE:</div><div class="line" id="LC1962">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;It is RECOMMENDED that only Operators be allowed to kill other users</div><div class="line" id="LC1963">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with KILL command.  This command has been the subject of many</div><div class="line" id="LC1964">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;controversies over the years, and along with the above</div><div class="line" id="LC1965">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;recommendation, it is also widely recognized that not even operators</div><div class="line" id="LC1966">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;should be allowed to kill users on remote servers.</div><div class="line" id="LC1967">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1968">3.7.2 Ping message</div><div class="line" id="LC1969">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1970">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: PING</div><div class="line" id="LC1971">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;server1&gt; [ &lt;server2&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC1972">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1973">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The PING command is used to test the presence of an active client or</div><div class="line" id="LC1974">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server at the other end of the connection.  Servers send a PING</div><div class="line" id="LC1975">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message at regular intervals if no other activity detected coming</div><div class="line" id="LC1976">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from a connection.  If a connection fails to respond to a PING</div><div class="line" id="LC1977">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message within a set amount of time, that connection is closed.  A</div><div class="line" id="LC1978">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PING message MAY be sent even if the connection is active.</div><div class="line" id="LC1979">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1980">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When a PING message is received, the appropriate PONG message MUST be</div><div class="line" id="LC1981">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent as reply to &lt;server1&gt; (server which sent the PING message out)</div><div class="line" id="LC1982">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;as soon as possible.  If the &lt;server2&gt; parameter is specified, it</div><div class="line" id="LC1983">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;represents the target of the ping, and the message gets forwarded</div><div class="line" id="LC1984">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;there.</div><div class="line" id="LC1985">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1986">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC1987">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1988">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOORIGIN                  ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC1989">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1990">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC1991">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1992">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PING tolsun.oulu.fi             ; Command to send a PING message to</div><div class="line" id="LC1993">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server</div><div class="line" id="LC1994">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1995">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PING WiZ tolsun.oulu.fi         ; Command from WiZ to send a PING</div><div class="line" id="LC1996">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message to server &quot;tolsun.oulu.fi&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC1997">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC1998">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PING :irc.funet.fi              ; Ping message sent by server</div><div class="line" id="LC1999">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;irc.funet.fi&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2000">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2001">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2002">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2003">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2004">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2005">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2006">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2007">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2008">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2009">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2010">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2011">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2012">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 36]</div><div class="line" id="LC2013">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2014">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2015">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2016">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2017">3.7.3 Pong message</div><div class="line" id="LC2018">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2019">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: PONG</div><div class="line" id="LC2020">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;server&gt; [ &lt;server2&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC2021">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2022">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PONG message is a reply to ping message.  If parameter &lt;server2&gt; is</div><div class="line" id="LC2023">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;given, this message MUST be forwarded to given target.  The &lt;server&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2024">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;parameter is the name of the entity who has responded to PING message</div><div class="line" id="LC2025">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and generated this message.</div><div class="line" id="LC2026">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2027">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2028">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2029">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOORIGIN                  ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC2030">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2031">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2032">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2033">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PONG csd.bu.edu tolsun.oulu.fi  ; PONG message from csd.bu.edu to</div><div class="line" id="LC2034">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;tolsun.oulu.fi</div><div class="line" id="LC2035">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2036">3.7.4 Error</div><div class="line" id="LC2037">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2038">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: ERROR</div><div class="line" id="LC2039">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;error message&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2040">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2041">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The ERROR command is for use by servers when reporting a serious or</div><div class="line" id="LC2042">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;fatal error to its peers.  It may also be sent from one server to</div><div class="line" id="LC2043">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;another but MUST NOT be accepted from any normal unknown clients.</div><div class="line" id="LC2044">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2045">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Only an ERROR message SHOULD be used for reporting errors which occur</div><div class="line" id="LC2046">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with a server-to-server link.  An ERROR message is sent to the server</div><div class="line" id="LC2047">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;at the other end (which reports it to appropriate local users and</div><div class="line" id="LC2048">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;logs) and to appropriate local users and logs.  It is not to be</div><div class="line" id="LC2049">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;passed onto any other servers by a server if it is received from a</div><div class="line" id="LC2050">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server.</div><div class="line" id="LC2051">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2052">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The ERROR message is also used before terminating a client</div><div class="line" id="LC2053">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connection.</div><div class="line" id="LC2054">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2055">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When a server sends a received ERROR message to its operators, the</div><div class="line" id="LC2056">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message SHOULD be encapsulated inside a NOTICE message, indicating</div><div class="line" id="LC2057">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;that the client was not responsible for the error.</div><div class="line" id="LC2058">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2059">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numerics:</div><div class="line" id="LC2060">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2061">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;None.</div><div class="line" id="LC2062">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2063">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2064">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2065">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2066">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2067">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2068">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 37]</div><div class="line" id="LC2069">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2070">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2071">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2072">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2073">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC2074">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2075">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERROR :Server *.fi already exists ; ERROR message to the other server</div><div class="line" id="LC2076">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which caused this error.</div><div class="line" id="LC2077">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2078">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOTICE WiZ :ERROR from csd.bu.edu -- Server *.fi already exists</div><div class="line" id="LC2079">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Same ERROR message as above but</div><div class="line" id="LC2080">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent to user WiZ on the other server.</div><div class="line" id="LC2081">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2082">4. Optional features</div><div class="line" id="LC2083">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2084">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This section describes OPTIONAL messages.  They are not required in a</div><div class="line" id="LC2085">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;working server implementation of the protocol described herein.  In</div><div class="line" id="LC2086">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the absence of the feature, an error reply message MUST be generated</div><div class="line" id="LC2087">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;or an unknown command error.  If the message is destined for another</div><div class="line" id="LC2088">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server to answer then it MUST be passed on (elementary parsing</div><div class="line" id="LC2089">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;REQUIRED) The allocated numerics for this are listed with the</div><div class="line" id="LC2090">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;messages below.</div><div class="line" id="LC2091">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2092">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From this section, only the USERHOST and ISON messages are available</div><div class="line" id="LC2093">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to services.</div><div class="line" id="LC2094">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2095">4.1 Away</div><div class="line" id="LC2096">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2097">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2098">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;text&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC2099">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2100">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With the AWAY command, clients can set an automatic reply string for</div><div class="line" id="LC2101">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;any PRIVMSG commands directed at them (not to a channel they are on).</div><div class="line" id="LC2102">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The server sends an automatic reply to the client sending the PRIVMSG</div><div class="line" id="LC2103">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command.  The only replying server is the one to which the sending</div><div class="line" id="LC2104">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;client is connected to.</div><div class="line" id="LC2105">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2106">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The AWAY command is used either with one parameter, to set an AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2107">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message, or with no parameters, to remove the AWAY message.</div><div class="line" id="LC2108">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2109">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Because of its high cost (memory and bandwidth wise), the AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2110">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message SHOULD only be used for client-server communication.  A</div><div class="line" id="LC2111">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server MAY choose to silently ignore AWAY messages received from</div><div class="line" id="LC2112">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other servers.  To update the away status of a client across servers,</div><div class="line" id="LC2113">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the user mode &#39;a&#39; SHOULD be used instead.  (See Section 3.1.5)</div><div class="line" id="LC2114">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2115">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2116">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2117">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_UNAWAY                    RPL_NOWAWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2118">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2119">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2120">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2121">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2122">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2123">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2124">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 38]</div><div class="line" id="LC2125">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2126">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2127">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2128">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2129">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2130">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2131">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;AWAY :Gone to lunch.  Back in 5 ; Command to set away message to</div><div class="line" id="LC2132">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Gone to lunch.  Back in 5&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC2133">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2134">4.2 Rehash message</div><div class="line" id="LC2135">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2136">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: REHASH</div><div class="line" id="LC2137">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: None</div><div class="line" id="LC2138">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2139">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The rehash command is an administrative command which can be used by</div><div class="line" id="LC2140">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;an operator to force the server to re-read and process its</div><div class="line" id="LC2141">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;configuration file.</div><div class="line" id="LC2142">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2143">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2144">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2145">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_REHASHING                 ERR_NOPRIVILEGES</div><div class="line" id="LC2146">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2147">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2148">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2149">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2150">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;REHASH                          ; message from user with operator</div><div class="line" id="LC2151">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;status to server asking it to reread</div><div class="line" id="LC2152">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;its configuration file.</div><div class="line" id="LC2153">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2154">4.3 Die message</div><div class="line" id="LC2155">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2156">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: DIE</div><div class="line" id="LC2157">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: None</div><div class="line" id="LC2158">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2159">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An operator can use the DIE command to shutdown the server.  This</div><div class="line" id="LC2160">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message is optional since it may be viewed as a risk to allow</div><div class="line" id="LC2161">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;arbitrary people to connect to a server as an operator and execute</div><div class="line" id="LC2162">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;this command.</div><div class="line" id="LC2163">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2164">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The DIE command MUST always be fully processed by the server to which</div><div class="line" id="LC2165">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the sending client is connected and MUST NOT be passed onto other</div><div class="line" id="LC2166">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connected servers.</div><div class="line" id="LC2167">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2168">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2169">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2170">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOPRIVILEGES</div><div class="line" id="LC2171">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2172">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2173">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2174">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;DIE                             ; no parameters required.</div><div class="line" id="LC2175">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2176">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2177">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2178">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2179">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2180">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 39]</div><div class="line" id="LC2181">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2182">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2183">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2184">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2185">4.4 Restart message</div><div class="line" id="LC2186">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2187">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: RESTART</div><div class="line" id="LC2188">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: None</div><div class="line" id="LC2189">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2190">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An operator can use the restart command to force the server to</div><div class="line" id="LC2191">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;restart itself.  This message is optional since it may be viewed as a</div><div class="line" id="LC2192">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;risk to allow arbitrary people to connect to a server as an operator</div><div class="line" id="LC2193">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and execute this command, causing (at least) a disruption to service.</div><div class="line" id="LC2194">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2195">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The RESTART command MUST always be fully processed by the server to</div><div class="line" id="LC2196">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which the sending client is connected and MUST NOT be passed onto</div><div class="line" id="LC2197">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;other connected servers.</div><div class="line" id="LC2198">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2199">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2200">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2201">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOPRIVILEGES</div><div class="line" id="LC2202">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2203">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2204">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2205">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RESTART                         ; no parameters required.</div><div class="line" id="LC2206">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2207">4.5 Summon message</div><div class="line" id="LC2208">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2209">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: SUMMON</div><div class="line" id="LC2210">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;user&gt; [ &lt;target&gt; [ &lt;channel&gt; ] ]</div><div class="line" id="LC2211">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2212">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SUMMON command can be used to give users who are on a host</div><div class="line" id="LC2213">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;running an IRC server a message asking them to please join IRC.  This</div><div class="line" id="LC2214">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message is only sent if the target server (a) has SUMMON enabled, (b)</div><div class="line" id="LC2215">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the user is logged in and (c) the server process can write to the</div><div class="line" id="LC2216">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;user&#39;s tty (or similar).</div><div class="line" id="LC2217">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2218">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If no &lt;server&gt; parameter is given it tries to summon &lt;user&gt; from the</div><div class="line" id="LC2219">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server the client is connected to is assumed as the target.</div><div class="line" id="LC2220">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2221">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If summon is not enabled in a server, it MUST return the</div><div class="line" id="LC2222">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_SUMMONDISABLED numeric.</div><div class="line" id="LC2223">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2224">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2225">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2226">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NORECIPIENT               ERR_FILEERROR</div><div class="line" id="LC2227">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOLOGIN                   ERR_NOSUCHSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC2228">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_SUMMONDISABLED            RPL_SUMMONING</div><div class="line" id="LC2229">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2230">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2231">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2232">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2233">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2234">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2235">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2236">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 40]</div><div class="line" id="LC2237">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2238">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2239">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2240">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2241">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Examples:</div><div class="line" id="LC2242">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2243">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SUMMON jto                      ; summon user jto on the server&#39;s</div><div class="line" id="LC2244">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;host</div><div class="line" id="LC2245">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2246">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SUMMON jto tolsun.oulu.fi       ; summon user jto on the host which a</div><div class="line" id="LC2247">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server named &quot;tolsun.oulu.fi&quot; is</div><div class="line" id="LC2248">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;running.</div><div class="line" id="LC2249">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2250">4.6 Users</div><div class="line" id="LC2251">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2252">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: USERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2253">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: [ &lt;target&gt; ]</div><div class="line" id="LC2254">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2255">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The USERS command returns a list of users logged into the server in a</div><div class="line" id="LC2256">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;format similar to the UNIX commands who(1), rusers(1) and finger(1).</div><div class="line" id="LC2257">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If disabled, the correct numeric MUST be returned to indicate this.</div><div class="line" id="LC2258">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2259">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Because of the security implications of such a command, it SHOULD be</div><div class="line" id="LC2260">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;disabled by default in server implementations.  Enabling it SHOULD</div><div class="line" id="LC2261">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;require recompiling the server or some equivalent change rather than</div><div class="line" id="LC2262">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;simply toggling an option and restarting the server.  The procedure</div><div class="line" id="LC2263">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to enable this command SHOULD also include suitable large comments.</div><div class="line" id="LC2264">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2265">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2266">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2267">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NOSUCHSERVER              ERR_FILEERROR</div><div class="line" id="LC2268">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_USERSSTART                RPL_USERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2269">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NOUSERS                   RPL_ENDOFUSERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2270">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_USERSDISABLED</div><div class="line" id="LC2271">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2272">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Disabled Reply:</div><div class="line" id="LC2273">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2274">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_USERSDISABLED</div><div class="line" id="LC2275">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2276">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2277">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2278">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;USERS eff.org                   ; request a list of users logged in</div><div class="line" id="LC2279">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;on server eff.org</div><div class="line" id="LC2280">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2281">4.7 Operwall message</div><div class="line" id="LC2282">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2283">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: WALLOPS</div><div class="line" id="LC2284">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;Text to be sent&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2285">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2286">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The WALLOPS command is used to send a message to all currently</div><div class="line" id="LC2287">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connected users who have set the &#39;w&#39; user mode for themselves.  (See</div><div class="line" id="LC2288">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section 3.1.5 &quot;User modes&quot;).</div><div class="line" id="LC2289">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2290">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2291">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2292">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 41]</div><div class="line" id="LC2293">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2294">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2295">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2296">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2297">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After implementing WALLOPS as a user command it was found that it was</div><div class="line" id="LC2298">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;often and commonly abused as a means of sending a message to a lot of</div><div class="line" id="LC2299">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;people.  Due to this, it is RECOMMENDED that the implementation of</div><div class="line" id="LC2300">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WALLOPS allows and recognizes only servers as the originators of</div><div class="line" id="LC2301">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WALLOPS.</div><div class="line" id="LC2302">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2303">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2304">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2305">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS</div><div class="line" id="LC2306">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2307">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2308">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2309">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:csd.bu.edu WALLOPS :Connect &#39;*.uiuc.edu 6667&#39; from Joshua ; WALLOPS</div><div class="line" id="LC2310">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message from csd.bu.edu announcing a</div><div class="line" id="LC2311">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CONNECT message it received from</div><div class="line" id="LC2312">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Joshua and acted upon.</div><div class="line" id="LC2313">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2314">4.8 Userhost message</div><div class="line" id="LC2315">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2316">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: USERHOST</div><div class="line" id="LC2317">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;nickname&gt; *( SPACE &lt;nickname&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC2318">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2319">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The USERHOST command takes a list of up to 5 nicknames, each</div><div class="line" id="LC2320">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;separated by a space character and returns a list of information</div><div class="line" id="LC2321">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;about each nickname that it found.  The returned list has each reply</div><div class="line" id="LC2322">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;separated by a space.</div><div class="line" id="LC2323">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2324">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2325">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2326">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_USERHOST                  ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS</div><div class="line" id="LC2327">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2328">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2329">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2330">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;USERHOST Wiz Michael syrk       ; USERHOST request for information on</div><div class="line" id="LC2331">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;nicks &quot;Wiz&quot;, &quot;Michael&quot;, and &quot;syrk&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2332">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2333">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:ircd.stealth.net 302 yournick :syrk=+syrk@millennium.stealth.net</div><div class="line" id="LC2334">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Reply for user syrk</div><div class="line" id="LC2335">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2336">4.9 Ison message</div><div class="line" id="LC2337">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2338">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Command: ISON</div><div class="line" id="LC2339">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parameters: &lt;nickname&gt; *( SPACE &lt;nickname&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC2340">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2341">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The ISON command was implemented to provide a quick and efficient</div><div class="line" id="LC2342">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;means to get a response about whether a given nickname was currently</div><div class="line" id="LC2343">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;on IRC. ISON only takes one (1) type of parameter: a space-separated</div><div class="line" id="LC2344">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;list of nicks.  For each nickname in the list that is present, the</div><div class="line" id="LC2345">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2346">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2347">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2348">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 42]</div><div class="line" id="LC2349">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2350">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2351">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2352">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2353">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server adds that to its reply string.  Thus the reply string may</div><div class="line" id="LC2354">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return empty (none of the given nicks are present), an exact copy of</div><div class="line" id="LC2355">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the parameter string (all of them present) or any other subset of the</div><div class="line" id="LC2356">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;set of nicks given in the parameter.  The only limit on the number of</div><div class="line" id="LC2357">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;nicks that may be checked is that the combined length MUST NOT be too</div><div class="line" id="LC2358">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;large as to cause the server to chop it off so it fits in 512</div><div class="line" id="LC2359">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;characters.</div><div class="line" id="LC2360">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2361">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ISON is only processed by the server local to the client sending the</div><div class="line" id="LC2362">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command and thus not passed onto other servers for further</div><div class="line" id="LC2363">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;processing.</div><div class="line" id="LC2364">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2365">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numeric Replies:</div><div class="line" id="LC2366">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2367">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ISON                      ERR_NEEDMOREPARAMS</div><div class="line" id="LC2368">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2369">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Example:</div><div class="line" id="LC2370">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2371">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ISON phone trillian WiZ jarlek Avalon Angel Monstah syrk</div><div class="line" id="LC2372">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;; Sample ISON request for 7 nicks.</div><div class="line" id="LC2373">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2374">5. Replies</div><div class="line" id="LC2375">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2376">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The following is a list of numeric replies which are generated in</div><div class="line" id="LC2377">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;response to the commands given above.  Each numeric is given with its</div><div class="line" id="LC2378">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;number, name and reply string.</div><div class="line" id="LC2379">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2380">5.1 Command responses</div><div class="line" id="LC2381">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2382">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Numerics in the range from 001 to 099 are used for client-server</div><div class="line" id="LC2383">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;connections only and should never travel between servers.  Replies</div><div class="line" id="LC2384">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;generated in the response to commands are found in the range from 200</div><div class="line" id="LC2385">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to 399.</div><div class="line" id="LC2386">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2387">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;001    RPL_WELCOME</div><div class="line" id="LC2388">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Welcome to the Internet Relay Network</div><div class="line" id="LC2389">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;nick&gt;!&lt;user&gt;@&lt;host&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2390">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;002    RPL_YOURHOST</div><div class="line" id="LC2391">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Your host is &lt;servername&gt;, running version &lt;ver&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2392">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;003    RPL_CREATED</div><div class="line" id="LC2393">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;This server was created &lt;date&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2394">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;004    RPL_MYINFO</div><div class="line" id="LC2395">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;servername&gt; &lt;version&gt; &lt;available user modes&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2396">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;available channel modes&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2397">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2398">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- The server sends Replies 001 to 004 to a user upon</div><div class="line" id="LC2399">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;successful registration.</div><div class="line" id="LC2400">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2401">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2402">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2403">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2404">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 43]</div><div class="line" id="LC2405">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2406">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2407">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2408">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2409">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;005    RPL_BOUNCE</div><div class="line" id="LC2410">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Try server &lt;server name&gt;, port &lt;port number&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2411">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2412">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Sent by the server to a user to suggest an alternative</div><div class="line" id="LC2413">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server.  This is often used when the connection is</div><div class="line" id="LC2414">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;refused because the server is already full.</div><div class="line" id="LC2415">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2416">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;302    RPL_USERHOST</div><div class="line" id="LC2417">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:*1&lt;reply&gt; *( &quot; &quot; &lt;reply&gt; )&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2418">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2419">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Reply format used by USERHOST to list replies to</div><div class="line" id="LC2420">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the query list.  The reply string is composed as</div><div class="line" id="LC2421">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;follows:</div><div class="line" id="LC2422">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2423">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reply = nickname [ &quot;*&quot; ] &quot;=&quot; ( &quot;+&quot; / &quot;-&quot; ) hostname</div><div class="line" id="LC2424">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2425">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &#39;*&#39; indicates whether the client has registered</div><div class="line" id="LC2426">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;as an Operator.  The &#39;-&#39; or &#39;+&#39; characters represent</div><div class="line" id="LC2427">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;whether the client has set an AWAY message or not</div><div class="line" id="LC2428">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;respectively.</div><div class="line" id="LC2429">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2430">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;303    RPL_ISON</div><div class="line" id="LC2431">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:*1&lt;nick&gt; *( &quot; &quot; &lt;nick&gt; )&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2432">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2433">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Reply format used by ISON to list replies to the</div><div class="line" id="LC2434">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;query list.</div><div class="line" id="LC2435">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2436">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;301    RPL_AWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2437">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; :&lt;away message&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2438">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;305    RPL_UNAWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2439">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:You are no longer marked as being away&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2440">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;306    RPL_NOWAWAY</div><div class="line" id="LC2441">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:You have been marked as being away&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2442">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2443">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- These replies are used with the AWAY command (if</div><div class="line" id="LC2444">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;allowed).  RPL_AWAY is sent to any client sending a</div><div class="line" id="LC2445">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PRIVMSG to a client which is away.  RPL_AWAY is only</div><div class="line" id="LC2446">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent by the server to which the client is connected.</div><div class="line" id="LC2447">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Replies RPL_UNAWAY and RPL_NOWAWAY are sent when the</div><div class="line" id="LC2448">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;client removes and sets an AWAY message.</div><div class="line" id="LC2449">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2450">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;311    RPL_WHOISUSER</div><div class="line" id="LC2451">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; &lt;user&gt; &lt;host&gt; * :&lt;real name&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2452">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;312    RPL_WHOISSERVER</div><div class="line" id="LC2453">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; &lt;server&gt; :&lt;server info&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2454">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;313    RPL_WHOISOPERATOR</div><div class="line" id="LC2455">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; :is an IRC operator&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2456">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2457">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2458">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2459">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2460">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 44]</div><div class="line" id="LC2461">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2462">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2463">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2464">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2465">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;317    RPL_WHOISIDLE</div><div class="line" id="LC2466">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; &lt;integer&gt; :seconds idle&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2467">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;318    RPL_ENDOFWHOIS</div><div class="line" id="LC2468">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; :End of WHOIS list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2469">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;319    RPL_WHOISCHANNELS</div><div class="line" id="LC2470">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; :*( ( &quot;@&quot; / &quot;+&quot; ) &lt;channel&gt; &quot; &quot; )&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2471">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2472">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Replies 311 - 313, 317 - 319 are all replies</div><div class="line" id="LC2473">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;generated in response to a WHOIS message.  Given that</div><div class="line" id="LC2474">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;there are enough parameters present, the answering</div><div class="line" id="LC2475">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server MUST either formulate a reply out of the above</div><div class="line" id="LC2476">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;numerics (if the query nick is found) or return an</div><div class="line" id="LC2477">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;error reply.  The &#39;*&#39; in RPL_WHOISUSER is there as</div><div class="line" id="LC2478">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the literal character and not as a wild card.  For</div><div class="line" id="LC2479">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each reply set, only RPL_WHOISCHANNELS may appear</div><div class="line" id="LC2480">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;more than once (for long lists of channel names).</div><div class="line" id="LC2481">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &#39;@&#39; and &#39;+&#39; characters next to the channel name</div><div class="line" id="LC2482">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;indicate whether a client is a channel operator or</div><div class="line" id="LC2483">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;has been granted permission to speak on a moderated</div><div class="line" id="LC2484">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channel.  The RPL_ENDOFWHOIS reply is used to mark</div><div class="line" id="LC2485">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the end of processing a WHOIS message.</div><div class="line" id="LC2486">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2487">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;314    RPL_WHOWASUSER</div><div class="line" id="LC2488">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; &lt;user&gt; &lt;host&gt; * :&lt;real name&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2489">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;369    RPL_ENDOFWHOWAS</div><div class="line" id="LC2490">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nick&gt; :End of WHOWAS&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2491">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2492">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When replying to a WHOWAS message, a server MUST use</div><div class="line" id="LC2493">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the replies RPL_WHOWASUSER, RPL_WHOISSERVER or</div><div class="line" id="LC2494">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ERR_WASNOSUCHNICK for each nickname in the presented</div><div class="line" id="LC2495">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;list.  At the end of all reply batches, there MUST</div><div class="line" id="LC2496">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;be RPL_ENDOFWHOWAS (even if there was only one reply</div><div class="line" id="LC2497">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and it was an error).</div><div class="line" id="LC2498">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2499">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;321    RPL_LISTSTART</div><div class="line" id="LC2500">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Obsolete. Not used.</div><div class="line" id="LC2501">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2502">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;322    RPL_LIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2503">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;# visible&gt; :&lt;topic&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2504">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;323    RPL_LISTEND</div><div class="line" id="LC2505">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:End of LIST&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2506">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2507">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Replies RPL_LIST, RPL_LISTEND mark the actual replies</div><div class="line" id="LC2508">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with data and end of the server&#39;s response to a LIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2509">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command.  If there are no channels available to return,</div><div class="line" id="LC2510">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;only the end reply MUST be sent.</div><div class="line" id="LC2511">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2512">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2513">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2514">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2515">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2516">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 45]</div><div class="line" id="LC2517">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2518">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2519">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2520">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2521">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;325    RPL_UNIQOPIS</div><div class="line" id="LC2522">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;nickname&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2523">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2524">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;324    RPL_CHANNELMODEIS</div><div class="line" id="LC2525">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;mode&gt; &lt;mode params&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2526">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2527">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;331    RPL_NOTOPIC</div><div class="line" id="LC2528">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; :No topic is set&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2529">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;332    RPL_TOPIC</div><div class="line" id="LC2530">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; :&lt;topic&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2531">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2532">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When sending a TOPIC message to determine the</div><div class="line" id="LC2533">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channel topic, one of two replies is sent.  If</div><div class="line" id="LC2534">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the topic is set, RPL_TOPIC is sent back else</div><div class="line" id="LC2535">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NOTOPIC.</div><div class="line" id="LC2536">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2537">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;341    RPL_INVITING</div><div class="line" id="LC2538">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;nick&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2539">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2540">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Returned by the server to indicate that the</div><div class="line" id="LC2541">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;attempted INVITE message was successful and is</div><div class="line" id="LC2542">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;being passed onto the end client.</div><div class="line" id="LC2543">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2544">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;342    RPL_SUMMONING</div><div class="line" id="LC2545">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;user&gt; :Summoning user to IRC&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2546">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2547">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Returned by a server answering a SUMMON message to</div><div class="line" id="LC2548">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;indicate that it is summoning that user.</div><div class="line" id="LC2549">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2550">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;346    RPL_INVITELIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2551">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;invitemask&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2552">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;347    RPL_ENDOFINVITELIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2553">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; :End of channel invite list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2554">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2555">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When listing the &#39;invitations masks&#39; for a given channel,</div><div class="line" id="LC2556">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a server is required to send the list back using the</div><div class="line" id="LC2557">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_INVITELIST and RPL_ENDOFINVITELIST messages.  A</div><div class="line" id="LC2558">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;separate RPL_INVITELIST is sent for each active mask.</div><div class="line" id="LC2559">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After the masks have been listed (or if none present) a</div><div class="line" id="LC2560">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFINVITELIST MUST be sent.</div><div class="line" id="LC2561">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2562">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;348    RPL_EXCEPTLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2563">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;exceptionmask&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2564">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;349    RPL_ENDOFEXCEPTLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2565">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; :End of channel exception list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2566">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2567">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2568">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2569">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2570">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2571">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2572">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 46]</div><div class="line" id="LC2573">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2574">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2575">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2576">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2577">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When listing the &#39;exception masks&#39; for a given channel,</div><div class="line" id="LC2578">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a server is required to send the list back using the</div><div class="line" id="LC2579">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_EXCEPTLIST and RPL_ENDOFEXCEPTLIST messages.  A</div><div class="line" id="LC2580">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;separate RPL_EXCEPTLIST is sent for each active mask.</div><div class="line" id="LC2581">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After the masks have been listed (or if none present)</div><div class="line" id="LC2582">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a RPL_ENDOFEXCEPTLIST MUST be sent.</div><div class="line" id="LC2583">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2584">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;351    RPL_VERSION</div><div class="line" id="LC2585">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;version&gt;.&lt;debuglevel&gt; &lt;server&gt; :&lt;comments&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2586">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2587">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Reply by the server showing its version details.</div><div class="line" id="LC2588">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &lt;version&gt; is the version of the software being</div><div class="line" id="LC2589">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;used (including any patchlevel revisions) and the</div><div class="line" id="LC2590">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;debuglevel&gt; is used to indicate if the server is</div><div class="line" id="LC2591">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;running in &quot;debug mode&quot;.</div><div class="line" id="LC2592">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2593">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The &quot;comments&quot; field may contain any comments about</div><div class="line" id="LC2594">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the version or further version details.</div><div class="line" id="LC2595">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2596">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;352    RPL_WHOREPLY</div><div class="line" id="LC2597">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;user&gt; &lt;host&gt; &lt;server&gt; &lt;nick&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2598">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;( &quot;H&quot; / &quot;G&quot; &gt; [&quot;*&quot;] [ ( &quot;@&quot; / &quot;+&quot; ) ]</div><div class="line" id="LC2599">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:&lt;hopcount&gt; &lt;real name&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2600">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2601">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;315    RPL_ENDOFWHO</div><div class="line" id="LC2602">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;name&gt; :End of WHO list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2603">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2604">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- The RPL_WHOREPLY and RPL_ENDOFWHO pair are used</div><div class="line" id="LC2605">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to answer a WHO message.  The RPL_WHOREPLY is only</div><div class="line" id="LC2606">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent if there is an appropriate match to the WHO</div><div class="line" id="LC2607">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;query.  If there is a list of parameters supplied</div><div class="line" id="LC2608">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with a WHO message, a RPL_ENDOFWHO MUST be sent</div><div class="line" id="LC2609">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;after processing each list item with &lt;name&gt; being</div><div class="line" id="LC2610">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the item.</div><div class="line" id="LC2611">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2612">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;353    RPL_NAMREPLY</div><div class="line" id="LC2613">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;( &quot;=&quot; / &quot;*&quot; / &quot;@&quot; ) &lt;channel&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2614">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:[ &quot;@&quot; / &quot;+&quot; ] &lt;nick&gt; *( &quot; &quot; [ &quot;@&quot; / &quot;+&quot; ] &lt;nick&gt; )</div><div class="line" id="LC2615">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- &quot;@&quot; is used for secret channels, &quot;*&quot; for private</div><div class="line" id="LC2616">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channels, and &quot;=&quot; for others (public channels).</div><div class="line" id="LC2617">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2618">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;366    RPL_ENDOFNAMES</div><div class="line" id="LC2619">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; :End of NAMES list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2620">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2621">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- To reply to a NAMES message, a reply pair consisting</div><div class="line" id="LC2622">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of RPL_NAMREPLY and RPL_ENDOFNAMES is sent by the</div><div class="line" id="LC2623">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server back to the client.  If there is no channel</div><div class="line" id="LC2624">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;found as in the query, then only RPL_ENDOFNAMES is</div><div class="line" id="LC2625">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2626">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2627">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2628">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 47]</div><div class="line" id="LC2629">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2630">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2631">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2632">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2633">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;returned.  The exception to this is when a NAMES</div><div class="line" id="LC2634">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message is sent with no parameters and all visible</div><div class="line" id="LC2635">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;channels and contents are sent back in a series of</div><div class="line" id="LC2636">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NAMEREPLY messages with a RPL_ENDOFNAMES to mark</div><div class="line" id="LC2637">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the end.</div><div class="line" id="LC2638">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2639">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;364    RPL_LINKS</div><div class="line" id="LC2640">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;mask&gt; &lt;server&gt; :&lt;hopcount&gt; &lt;server info&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2641">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;365    RPL_ENDOFLINKS</div><div class="line" id="LC2642">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;mask&gt; :End of LINKS list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2643">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2644">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- In replying to the LINKS message, a server MUST send</div><div class="line" id="LC2645">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;replies back using the RPL_LINKS numeric and mark the</div><div class="line" id="LC2646">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;end of the list using an RPL_ENDOFLINKS reply.</div><div class="line" id="LC2647">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2648">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;367    RPL_BANLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2649">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt; &lt;banmask&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2650">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;368    RPL_ENDOFBANLIST</div><div class="line" id="LC2651">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;channel&gt;
