:End of channel ban list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2652">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2653">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When listing the active &#39;bans&#39; for a given channel,</div><div class="line" id="LC2654">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a server is required to send the list back using the</div><div class="line" id="LC2655">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_BANLIST and RPL_ENDOFBANLIST messages.  A separate</div><div class="line" id="LC2656">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_BANLIST is sent for each active banmask.  After the</div><div class="line" id="LC2657">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;banmasks have been listed (or if none present) a</div><div class="line" id="LC2658">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFBANLIST MUST be sent.</div><div class="line" id="LC2659">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2660">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;371    RPL_INFO</div><div class="line" id="LC2661">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:&lt;string&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2662">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;374    RPL_ENDOFINFO</div><div class="line" id="LC2663">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:End of INFO list&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2664">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2665">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- A server responding to an INFO message is required to</div><div class="line" id="LC2666">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;send all its &#39;info&#39; in a series of RPL_INFO messages</div><div class="line" id="LC2667">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with a RPL_ENDOFINFO reply to indicate the end of the</div><div class="line" id="LC2668">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;replies.</div><div class="line" id="LC2669">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2670">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;375    RPL_MOTDSTART</div><div class="line" id="LC2671">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:- &lt;server&gt; Message of the day - &quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2672">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;372    RPL_MOTD</div><div class="line" id="LC2673">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:- &lt;text&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2674">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;376    RPL_ENDOFMOTD</div><div class="line" id="LC2675">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:End of MOTD command&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2676">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2677">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When responding to the MOTD message and the MOTD file</div><div class="line" id="LC2678">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is found, the file is displayed line by line, with</div><div class="line" id="LC2679">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each line no longer than 80 characters, using</div><div class="line" id="LC2680">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2681">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2682">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2683">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2684">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 48]</div><div class="line" id="LC2685">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2686">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2687">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2688">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2689">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_MOTD format replies.  These MUST be surrounded</div><div class="line" id="LC2690">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by a RPL_MOTDSTART (before the RPL_MOTDs) and an</div><div class="line" id="LC2691">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_ENDOFMOTD (after).</div><div class="line" id="LC2692">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2693">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;381    RPL_YOUREOPER</div><div class="line" id="LC2694">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:You are now an IRC operator&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2695">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2696">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- RPL_YOUREOPER is sent back to a client which has</div><div class="line" id="LC2697">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;just successfully issued an OPER message and gained</div><div class="line" id="LC2698">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;operator status.</div><div class="line" id="LC2699">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2700">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;382    RPL_REHASHING</div><div class="line" id="LC2701">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;config file&gt; :Rehashing&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2702">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2703">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- If the REHASH option is used and an operator sends</div><div class="line" id="LC2704">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a REHASH message, an RPL_REHASHING is sent back to</div><div class="line" id="LC2705">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the operator.</div><div class="line" id="LC2706">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2707">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;383    RPL_YOURESERVICE</div><div class="line" id="LC2708">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;You are service &lt;servicename&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2709">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2710">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- Sent by the server to a service upon successful</div><div class="line" id="LC2711">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;registration.</div><div class="line" id="LC2712">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2713">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;391    RPL_TIME</div><div class="line" id="LC2714">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;server&gt; :&lt;string showing server&#39;s local time&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2715">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2716">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When replying to the TIME message, a server MUST send</div><div class="line" id="LC2717">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the reply using the RPL_TIME format above.  The string</div><div class="line" id="LC2718">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;showing the time need only contain the correct day and</div><div class="line" id="LC2719">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;time there.  There is no further requirement for the</div><div class="line" id="LC2720">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;time string.</div><div class="line" id="LC2721">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2722">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;392    RPL_USERSSTART</div><div class="line" id="LC2723">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:UserID   Terminal  Host&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2724">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;393    RPL_USERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2725">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:&lt;username&gt; &lt;ttyline&gt; &lt;hostname&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2726">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;394    RPL_ENDOFUSERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2727">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:End of users&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2728">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;395    RPL_NOUSERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2729">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:Nobody logged in&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2730">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2731">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- If the USERS message is handled by a server, the</div><div class="line" id="LC2732">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;replies RPL_USERSTART, RPL_USERS, RPL_ENDOFUSERS and</div><div class="line" id="LC2733">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_NOUSERS are used.  RPL_USERSSTART MUST be sent</div><div class="line" id="LC2734">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;first, following by either a sequence of RPL_USERS</div><div class="line" id="LC2735">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;or a single RPL_NOUSER. &lt;backstream sendq&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2749">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;upstream sendq&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2750">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;201    RPL_TRACECONNECTING</div><div class="line" id="LC2751">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;Try. &lt;class&gt; How many are</div><div class="line" id="LC2778">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;returned is dependent on the TRACE message and</div><div class="line" id="LC2779">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;whether it was sent by an operator or not.  There</div><div class="line" id="LC2780">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is no predefined order for which occurs first.</div><div class="line" id="LC2781">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Replies RPL_TRACEUNKNOWN, RPL_TRACECONNECTING and</div><div class="line" id="LC2782">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACEHANDSHAKE are all used for connections</div><div class="line" id="LC2783">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which have not been fully established and are either</div><div class="line" id="LC2784">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;unknown, still attempting to connect or in the</div><div class="line" id="LC2785">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;process of completing the &#39;server handshake&#39;.</div><div class="line" id="LC2786">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACELINK is sent by any server which handles</div><div class="line" id="LC2787">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a TRACE message and has to pass it on to another</div><div class="line" id="LC2788">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server.  The list of RPL_TRACELINKs sent in</div><div class="line" id="LC2789">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;response to a TRACE command traversing the IRC</div><div class="line" id="LC2790">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;network should reflect the actual connectivity of</div><div class="line" id="LC2791">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the servers themselves along that path.</div><div class="line" id="LC2792">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2793">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2794">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2795">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2796">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 50]</div><div class="line" id="LC2797">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2798">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2799">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2800">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2801">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACENEWTYPE is to be used for any connection</div><div class="line" id="LC2802">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;which does not fit in the other categories but is</div><div class="line" id="LC2803">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;being displayed anyway.</div><div class="line" id="LC2804">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_TRACEEND is sent to indicate the end of the list.</div><div class="line" id="LC2805">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2806">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;211    RPL_STATSLINKINFO</div><div class="line" id="LC2807">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;linkname&gt; &lt;sendq&gt; &lt;sent messages&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2808">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;sent Kbytes&gt; &lt;received messages&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2809">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;received Kbytes&gt; &lt;time open&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2810">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2811">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- reports statistics on a connection.  &lt;linkname&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2812">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;identifies the particular connection, &lt;sendq&gt; is</div><div class="line" id="LC2813">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the amount of data that is queued and waiting to be</div><div class="line" id="LC2814">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sent &lt;sent messages&gt; the number of messages sent,</div><div class="line" id="LC2815">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and &lt;sent Kbytes&gt; the amount of data sent, in</div><div class="line" id="LC2816">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Kbytes. &lt;received messages&gt; and &lt;received Kbytes&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2817">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;are the equivalent of &lt;sent messages&gt; and &lt;sent</div><div class="line" id="LC2818">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Kbytes&gt; for received data, respectively.  &lt;time</div><div class="line" id="LC2819">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;open&gt; indicates how long ago the connection was</div><div class="line" id="LC2820">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;opened, in seconds.</div><div class="line" id="LC2821">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2822">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;212    RPL_STATSCOMMANDS</div><div class="line" id="LC2823">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;command&gt; &lt;type&gt; :End of service listing&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2859">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2860">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When listing services in reply to a SERVLIST message,</div><div class="line" id="LC2861">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a server is required to send the list back using the</div><div class="line" id="LC2862">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_SERVLIST and RPL_SERVLISTEND messages.  A separate</div><div class="line" id="LC2863">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_SERVLIST is sent for each service.  After the</div><div class="line" id="LC2864">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;services have been listed (or if none present) a</div><div class="line" id="LC2865">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_SERVLISTEND MUST be sent.</div><div class="line" id="LC2866">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2867">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;251    RPL_LUSERCLIENT</div><div class="line" id="LC2868">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:There are &lt;integer&gt; users and &lt;integer&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2869">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;services on &lt;integer&gt; servers&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2870">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;252    RPL_LUSEROP</div><div class="line" id="LC2871">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;integer&gt; :operator(s) online&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2872">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;253    RPL_LUSERUNKNOWN</div><div class="line" id="LC2873">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;integer&gt; :unknown connection(s)&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2874">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;254    RPL_LUSERCHANNELS</div><div class="line" id="LC2875">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;integer&gt; :channels formed&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2876">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;255    RPL_LUSERME</div><div class="line" id="LC2877">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:I have &lt;integer&gt; clients and &lt;integer&gt;</div><div class="line" id="LC2878">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;servers&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2879">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2880">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- In processing an LUSERS message, the server</div><div class="line" id="LC2881">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;sends a set of replies from RPL_LUSERCLIENT,</div><div class="line" id="LC2882">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSEROP, RPL_USERUNKNOWN,</div><div class="line" id="LC2883">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSERCHANNELS and RPL_LUSERME.  When</div><div class="line" id="LC2884">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;replying, a server MUST send back</div><div class="line" id="LC2885">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;RPL_LUSERCLIENT and RPL_LUSERME.  The other</div><div class="line" id="LC2886">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;replies are only sent back if a non-zero count</div><div class="line" id="LC2887">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is found for them.</div><div class="line" id="LC2888">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2889">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;256    RPL_ADMINME</div><div class="line" id="LC2890">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;server&gt; :Administrative info&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2891">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;257    RPL_ADMINLOC1</div><div class="line" id="LC2892">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:&lt;admin info&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2893">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;258    RPL_ADMINLOC2</div><div class="line" id="LC2894">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:&lt;admin info&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2895">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;259    RPL_ADMINEMAIL</div><div class="line" id="LC2896">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;:&lt;admin info&gt;&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2897">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2898">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When replying to an ADMIN message, a server</div><div class="line" id="LC2899">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is expected to use replies RPL_ADMINME</div><div class="line" id="LC2900">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;through to RPL_ADMINEMAIL and provide a text</div><div class="line" id="LC2901">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;message with each.  For RPL_ADMINLOC1 a</div><div class="line" id="LC2902">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;description of what city, state and country</div><div class="line" id="LC2903">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the server is in is expected, followed by</div><div class="line" id="LC2904">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;details of the institution (RPL_ADMINLOC2)</div><div class="line" id="LC2905">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2906">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2907">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2908">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 52]</div><div class="line" id="LC2909">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2910">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC2911">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2912">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2913">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and finally the administrative contact for the</div><div class="line" id="LC2914">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server (an email address here is REQUIRED)</div><div class="line" id="LC2915">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in RPL_ADMINEMAIL.</div><div class="line" id="LC2916">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2917">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;263    RPL_TRYAGAIN</div><div class="line" id="LC2918">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;command&gt; :Please wait a while and try again.&quot;</div><div class="line" id="LC2919">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2920">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;- When a server drops a command without processing it,</div><div class="line" id="LC2921">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;it MUST use the reply RPL_TRYAGAIN to inform the</div><div class="line" id="LC2922">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;originating client.</div><div class="line" id="LC2923">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2924">5.2 Error Replies</div><div class="line" id="LC2925">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2926">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Error replies are found in the range from 400 to 599.</div><div class="line" id="LC2927">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC2928">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;401    ERR_NOSUCHNICK</div><div class="line" id="LC2929">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;&lt;nickname&gt; use;</div><div class="line" id="LC3296">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3297">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3298">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3299">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3300">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 59]</div><div class="line" id="LC3301">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3302">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC3303">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3304">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3305">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. reserved for future planned use;</div><div class="line" id="LC3306">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3307">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. in current use but are part of a non-generic &#39;feature&#39; of</div><div class="line" id="LC3308">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the current IRC server.</div><div class="line" id="LC3309">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3310">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;231    RPL_SERVICEINFO     232  RPL_ENDOFSERVICES</div><div class="line" id="LC3311">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;233    RPL_SERVICE</div><div class="line" id="LC3312">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;300    RPL_NONE            316  RPL_WHOISCHANOP</div><div class="line" id="LC3313">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;361    RPL_KILLDONE        362  RPL_CLOSING</div><div class="line" id="LC3314">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;363    RPL_CLOSEEND        373  RPL_INFOSTART</div><div class="line" id="LC3315">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;384    RPL_MYPORTIS</div><div class="line" id="LC3316">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3317">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;213    RPL_STATSCLINE      214  RPL_STATSNLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3318">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;215    RPL_STATSILINE      216  RPL_STATSKLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3319">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;217    RPL_STATSQLINE      218  RPL_STATSYLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3320">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;240    RPL_STATSVLINE      241  RPL_STATSLLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3321">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;244    RPL_STATSHLINE      244  RPL_STATSSLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3322">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;246    RPL_STATSPING       247  RPL_STATSBLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3323">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;250    RPL_STATSDLINE</div><div class="line" id="LC3324">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3325">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;492    ERR_NOSERVICEHOST</div><div class="line" id="LC3326">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3327">6. Current implementations</div><div class="line" id="LC3328">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3329">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The IRC software, version 2.10 is the only complete implementation of</div><div class="line" id="LC3330">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the IRC protocol (client and server).  Because of the small amount of</div><div class="line" id="LC3331">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;changes in the client protocol since the publication of RFC 1459</div><div class="line" id="LC3332">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[IRC], implementations that follow it are likely to be compliant with</div><div class="line" id="LC3333">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;this protocol or to require a small amount of changes to reach</div><div class="line" id="LC3334">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;compliance.</div><div class="line" id="LC3335">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3336">7. Current problems</div><div class="line" id="LC3337">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3338">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;There are a number of recognized problems with the IRC Client</div><div class="line" id="LC3339">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Protocol, and more generally with the IRC Server Protocol.  In order</div><div class="line" id="LC3340">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to preserve backward compatibility with old clients, this protocol</div><div class="line" id="LC3341">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;has almost not evolved since the publication of RFC 1459 [IRC].</div><div class="line" id="LC3342">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3343">7.1 Nicknames</div><div class="line" id="LC3344">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3345">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The idea of the nickname on IRC is very convenient for users to use</div><div class="line" id="LC3346">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;when talking to each other outside of a channel, but there is only a</div><div class="line" id="LC3347">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;finite nickname space and being what they are, it&#39;s not uncommon for</div><div class="line" id="LC3348">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;several people to want to use the same nick.  If a nickname is chosen</div><div class="line" id="LC3349">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by two people using this protocol, either one will not succeed or</div><div class="line" id="LC3350">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;both will removed by use of a server KILL (See Section 3.7.1).</div><div class="line" id="LC3351">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3352">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3353">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3354">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3355">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3356">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 60]</div><div class="line" id="LC3357">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3358">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC3359">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3360">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3361">7.2 Limitation of wildcards</div><div class="line" id="LC3362">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3363">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;There is no way to escape the escape character &quot;\&quot; (%x5C).  While</div><div class="line" id="LC3364">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;this isn&#39;t usually a problem, it makes it impossible to form a mask</div><div class="line" id="LC3365">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;with a backslash character (&quot;\&quot;) preceding a wildcard.</div><div class="line" id="LC3366">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3367">7.3 Security considerations</div><div class="line" id="LC3368">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3369">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Security issues related to this protocol are discussed in the &quot;IRC</div><div class="line" id="LC3370">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Server Protocol&quot; [IRC-SERVER] as they are mostly an issue for the</div><div class="line" id="LC3371">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;server side of the connection.</div><div class="line" id="LC3372">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3373">8. Current support and availability</div><div class="line" id="LC3374">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3375">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Mailing lists for IRC related discussion:</div><div class="line" id="LC3376">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;General discussion: ircd-users@irc.org</div><div class="line" id="LC3377">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Protocol development: ircd-dev@irc.org</div><div class="line" id="LC3378">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3379">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Software implementations:</div><div class="line" id="LC3380">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ftp://ftp.irc.org/irc/server</div><div class="line" id="LC3381">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ftp://ftp.funet.fi/pub/unix/irc</div><div class="line" id="LC3382">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ftp://ftp.irc.org/irc/clients</div><div class="line" id="LC3383">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3384">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Newsgroup: alt.irc</div><div class="line" id="LC3385">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3386">9. Acknowledgements</div><div class="line" id="LC3387">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3388">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Parts of this document were copied from the RFC 1459 [IRC] which</div><div class="line" id="LC3389">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;first formally documented the IRC Protocol.  It has also benefited</div><div class="line" id="LC3390">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;from many rounds of review and comments.  In particular, the</div><div class="line" id="LC3391">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;following people have made significant contributions to this</div><div class="line" id="LC3392">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;document:</div><div class="line" id="LC3393">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3394">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Matthew Green, Michael Neumayer, Volker Paulsen, Kurt Roeckx, Vesa</div><div class="line" id="LC3395">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Ruokonen, Magnus Tjernstrom, Stefan Zehl.</div><div class="line" id="LC3396">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3397">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3398">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3399">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3400">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3401">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3402">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3403">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3404">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3405">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3406">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3407">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3408">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3409">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3410">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3411">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3412">Kalt                         Informational                     [Page 61]</div><div class="line" id="LC3413">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3414">RFC 2812          Internet Relay Chat: Client Protocol        April 2000</div><div class="line" id="LC3415">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3416">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3417">10. References</div><div class="line" id="LC3418">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3419">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[KEYWORDS]   Bradner, S., &quot;Key words for use in RFCs to Indicate</div><div class="line" id="LC3420">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Requirement Levels&quot;, BCP 14, RFC 2119, March 1997.</div><div class="line" id="LC3421">&nbsp;</div><div class="line" id="LC3422">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[ABNF]       Crocker, D. and P.
